 Key points of the Bill: • Linking driving license and vehicle registration with Aadhaar-based platform to prevent de-duplication of license and registration of stolen vehicles
 • 'apatkaaleen vaahanon ko rasta nahin pradaan karne' par 10 hajaar rupee kaa jurmaana
 • Removal of cap on liability for third party insurance
 • driving license ke liye ek rashtriya register or 'vaahan' or 'sarathi' plateform ke madhyam se vaahan panjikaran ke liye ek rashtriya register banane kaa prastaav, taaki panjikaran or licencing kii prakriya ko sucharu banaaya ja sake
 Suggest such changes in the design of vehicles to make them suitable for persons with disabilities
 • motor vaahan durghatana kosh kaa nirmaan, jo nishchit prakaar ke durghatnaon ke liye bharat ke sabhi sadak upyogkartaaon ko anivaary beemaa cover pradaan karegaa
 • Construction of National Road Safety Board
 yah board, sadak suraksha or yatayaat prabandhan ke sabhi pahaluon par centre or rajya sarkaron ko salaah pradaan karegaa

 bharat ne pakistan kii ore se samjhauta express visphot ko mumbai hamale se jodne ke prayaas ko khaarij karte hue kaha ki yah thimpu main videsh sachiv str kii vaarta ko prabhavit karne kii koshish he
 Pakistan had said the delay in investigation of Samjhauta Express blast
 bharat kaa kahana he ki videsh sachiv str kii vaarta se pehle pakistan kii ore se is mulaakaat ko peeche kii ore le jane kaa prayaas he
 Official sources say that India's opinion is clear that both countries can move forward through negotiations
 videsh sachiv str kii vaarta kii purv sandhya par pakistan ne ek bhadakaau bayaan main kaha he ki samjhauta express visphot maamle main hindu aatankwaadiyon kii bhoomika kaa khulaasa karne ke sandarbh main bharat ke paas saahas kaa abhaav he
 Pakistan Foreign Ministry spokesman Abdul Basit said, "it seems that India lacks courage to disclose the conspiracy of Hindu terrorists and some people of Indian Army
" unhone kaha, varsh 2007 ke samjhauta express visphot maamle main bharat kii ab tak karrwai ummid ke mutabik nahin he
 India will have to eliminate the difference between words and actions
 pakistan main tamaato kii keemat aasmaan chhu rahi he
 a day before Eid Milad Un Nabi (eid-milad-ul-nabi), on Saturday, its price rose to Rs 160 to Rs 320 per kg in one day
 do din baad somvaar ko tamaato 140 se 170 rupee ke bhav par bik rahaa tha
 While the price of tomatoes has increased tremendously, people are having a lot of trouble, while housewives are considering the option of tomatoes in the kitchen
 tamaato ke daam badhane kii vajah se sthaneey dukandaaron ne thok bazaar se ise khareednaa band kar diya he, jisaki vajah se bazaaron main kritrim kami ho gai he
 Housewife Kulsum Bibi said that due to rising tomato prices, she is trying yogurt as an alternative
 vahiin ek anya gruhani farhat norin ne kaha ki unhen is samasya se kai baar do-chaar hona padaa he or ab unhone tarkeeb nikaali he ki jab daam kam ho zyada maatra main tamaato le liya jaae or use fries kar rakhaa jaae
 However, she says that the freeze stuff does not get the taste that is in fresh
 ek sthaneey vikreta abdul kareem ne kaha ki jamkhori or munafkhori kii vajah se tamaato ke daam bade hue hai
 Haji Shahjahan, president of the Wholesale Vegetable Dealers Association in Karachi, said that the arrival of tomatoes from Balochistan has been less and the tomatoes coming from Iran are also not reaching
 kabul se aane vaala tamaato bhi kisi kaaran se rukaa hua he
 He said that tomato crop usually arrives in October, but this time it has been delayed due to which prices have increased
 unhone kaha ki 15 se 20 din main aavak sudharne kii ummid he
 Opponents of the referendum in Greece, struggling to get out of the economic crisis, took out a rally, and surveys said that people's support for this move of the government was declining
 police ne kaha ki sarkaar ke samarthan main kareeb 25,000 logon ne raily nikaali or janata se aagrah kiya ki ravivaar ko hone vaale janamat sangrah main ve 'naa' ke paksh main matdaan karen
 About 20,000 people gathered at some distance from this rally venue to protest against the government and appealed to vote in favor of 'yes'
 pradhanmantri alexis sipraas logon se aagrah kar rahe hai ki ve janamat sangrah main euro kshetra ke karj se judi sharton ko nakaaren
 On the other hand, many Grecians are seen turning to 'yes' in view of the crisis and the possibility of deepening
 tippaniyan The European Union and the International Monetary Fund (IMF) pressured Greece ahead of the referendum and warned of the country's financial disrepair
 janamat sangrah euro kshetra main greece kaa bhavishya tay kar saktaa he
 The leftist government of Greece has placed its political future at stake on the referendum to be held on Sunday, however, the IMF warns that since the Syriza party has come to power in January, the country's growth prospects have dropped dramatically

 The referendum may decide Greece's future in the euro area
 greece kii vampanthi sarkaar ne ravivaar ko hone vaale janamat sangrah par apana raajnneetik bhavishya daanv par laga diya he, haalanki, idhar imef ne aagaah kiya he ki janvari main jab se sirija party satta main ai he desh kii vruddhi kii sambhaavna naatakeey rup se ghati he
